[6/12/2026 12:58 PM] Tupperbox#4754


{Embed}
Tupperbox
Tupperbox | Help (page 1/5 of 5 total results)
I am Tupperbox, a bot that allows you to send messages as other "profiles" called tuppers. Visit the [online guide](https://tupperbox.app/guide/basics) to learn the basics of making and sending messages as tuppers!

__**Getting Started**__
**tul!register** - Register a new tupper that you can send messages as
**tul!remove** - Remove a tupper from your account
**tul!list** - Get a list of your tuppers, or see someone else's
**tul!avatar** - Manage a tupper's avatar
**tul!rename** - Change a tupper's name
**tul!brackets** - Manage a tupper's brackets
**tul!dash** - Get a link to the Tupperbox Dashboard
​
Also check out these advanced topics:
**tul!help scopes** - Learn about scoped commands like ``tul!auto`` and ``tul!proxy``
**tul!help permissions** - Learn about Tupperbox permissions and how to manage them with ``tul!cfg``

Proxy tips:
React with ❌ to a proxy you've sent to delete it!
React with ❓ to a proxy to show who sent it in DM!
React with 📝 to edit a proxy you've sent!
*What's a proxy? It's a message sent as a tupper!*

You can also react with ❌ to any of my messages to delete them if you triggered them.

Try the [online dashboard](https://tupperbox.app/dashboard/list) for managing tuppers and settings. It can be easier than using Discord commands!
Invite me to your server --> [click](https://discord.com/oauth2/authorize?client_id=431544605209788416&scope=bot&permissions=536996928)
Questions? Join the support server: [invite](https://discord.gg/Z4BHccHhy3)

React to this message with ➡️ to see more commands.


[6/12/2026 7:16 PM] lizardpelt
tul!register


[6/12/2026 7:16 PM] Tupperbox#4754


{Embed}
Tupperbox
Tupperbox Command | register
Register a new tupper that you can send messages as

**Usage:**
**tul!register** _<name> <brackets>_ - Register a tupper named *<name>*.

If your tupper's name contains spaces, you must surround the full name in single or double quotes `'like this'` or `"like this"`.
You can upload an image when using this command to quickly set that image as the new tupper's avatar!

Your tupper's brackets must contain the exact word `text` with letters or symbols before or after it.
You can have brackets on one or both sides, like `r:text` or `>text<`.
The word `text` is a placeholder for what you want the tupper to say.
For example, if you run the command ``tul!register Example ex:text``, you would be able to make Example say "hello" by writing: `ex:hello`
<this> means required | [this] means optional | online guide: https://tupperbox.app/guide


[6/12/2026 7:21 PM] lizardpelt
tul!remove


[6/12/2026 7:21 PM] Tupperbox#4754


{Embed}
Tupperbox
Tupperbox Command | remove
Remove a tupper from your account

**Usage:**
**tul!remove** _<name>_ - Remove *<name>* from your account.
**tul!remove** _\*_ - Remove all of your tuppers (requires confirmation).
<this> means required | [this] means optional | online guide: https://tupperbox.app/guide

DISBOARD: The Public Server List
Hi! I am a bot for DISBOARD (https://disboard.org)

COMMAND LIST

**`/help`**: This!
**`/bump`**: Bump this server.
**`/page`**: Get a link to the server's DISBOARD page.
**`/invite [channel]`**: Set invite to this channel. If [channel] is specified, create an invite for that channel. *(Admin only.)*

**How do I add my server to DISBOARD?**

1. Login on DISBOARD website,
2. Go to Dashboard,
3. Click "Add New Server"
Fill out your server info and save it. You will be redirected to Discord's authorization screen. If not, click the "Add Bot" button on the server edit page.

Need help? Join the [support server](https://discord.gg/kbQMsHZVwp).

[6/20/2026 3:53 PM] Tupperbox#4754


{Embed}
Tupperbox
Tupperbox | Help (page 1/5 of 5 total results)
I am Tupperbox, a bot that allows you to send messages as other "profiles" called tuppers. Visit the [online guide](https://tupperbox.app/guide/basics) to learn the basics of making and sending messages as tuppers!

__**Getting Started**__
**tul!register** - Register a new tupper that you can send messages as
**tul!remove** - Remove a tupper from your account
**tul!list** - Get a list of your tuppers, or see someone else's
**tul!avatar** - Manage a tupper's avatar
**tul!rename** - Change a tupper's name
**tul!brackets** - Manage a tupper's brackets
**tul!dash** - Get a link to the Tupperbox Dashboard
​
Also check out these advanced topics:
**tul!help scopes** - Learn about scoped commands like ``tul!auto`` and ``tul!proxy``
**tul!help permissions** - Learn about Tupperbox permissions and how to manage them with ``tul!cfg``

Proxy tips:
React with ❌ to a proxy you've sent to delete it!
React with ❓ to a proxy to show who sent it in DM!
React with 📝 to edit a proxy you've sent!
*What's a proxy? It's a message sent as a tupper!*

You can also react with ❌ to any of my messages to delete them if you triggered them.

Try the [online dashboard](https://tupperbox.app/dashboard/list) for managing tuppers and settings. It can be easier than using Discord commands!
Invite me to your server --> [click](https://discord.com/oauth2/authorize?client_id=431544605209788416&scope=bot&permissions=536996928)
Questions? Join the support server: [invite](https://discord.gg/Z4BHccHhy3)

React to this message with ➡️ to see more commands.

Tupperbox Command | rename
Change a tupper's name

**Usage:**
**tul!rename** _<name> <newname>_ - Set *<name>*'s name to *<newname>*.

Use single or double quotes around multi-word names `"like this"` or `'like this'`.
<this> means required | [this] means optional | online guide: https://tupperbox.app/guide

[6/22/2026 7:58 PM] Howlbert#0720


{Embed}
Eltanin — Character Sheet
Appearance
Rich earthy brown coat with creamy face and crown; deep chocolate back and shoulders fading to cream behind the shoulders and under the chest. Strong muscular huntress build. Stern calculating green eyes. Old gash above the left eye from an elk hunt - healed clean, no sight penalty. Often carries burrs and pine sap from border runs.
Personality
Loyal, observant, bold, quiet. Deeply loyal to Thistlehide and fiercely protective of wolves she holds dear. Bold on the hunt - takes risks to feed the den, not from recklessness. Reserved; rarely drops her walls. Values dedication and loyalty; little patience for laziness or liars.
Backstory
Born in Thistlehide during a storm; only pup in her litter to survive - littermates culled for deformity. Mother died of birth trauma. Raised by the den; spent puphood watching and stalking small prey instead of playing. Still distant as an adult but socializes when duty calls. Raised around Maw belief but is agnostic - not hostile, unconvinced, keeps doubt private. Avoids Twolegs and thunder-sticks; refuses to range near logging scars when shots carry on the wind.
Family
Mother (hunter, died at her birth). No surviving littermates. Father not in her life.
RP Sample
The nursery hush was wrong. Eltanin had been washing blood from her paws at the creek when fear-scent hit her - a pup missing from the moss nest. A caretaker burst out, voice cracking. Eltanin cut her off: "Left paw. Small. Heading toward the elder-stones." She was already moving into the bracken without waiting for permission. Boldness was doing first what the den could not afford to do second.
Open Plots
Twoleg activity on eastern patrol; private Maw doubt if rot-season worsens; mistaken for cold because of silence; quietly watches over a caretaker or pup she will not admit to guarding.

[6/23/2026 11:20 AM] Howlbert#0720


{Embed}
Mirewort; Character Sheet
Appearance
Lean and sinewy, built for crawling through cypress knees and sucking mud. Patchy olive-brown fur stained greenish-black from swamp tannins, with weeping bald spots where shelf-fungus has taken root. Pale, watery amber eyes, always slightly unfocused. Left half of muzzle scarred smooth from a rot-lung treatment gone wrong. Slight limp, favoring right foreleg — paw missing two toes (snapping turtle). When still, marsh grasses seem to grow toward him.
Personality
Patient, morbid, curious, detached, fervent. Speaks in a low, wet murmur. Never rushes — examines wounds from three angles before acting. Dark gallows humor; names each plant after a wolf he failed to save. Detachment is necessity, not cruelty. Feverishly devout beneath the stillness. Murkvein suspects his closeness to the Maw; Dusk watches his Belly-Rip visits. He does not explain himself to either.
Backstory
Born to a Bog-Born mother who died of milk-fever at three weeks. Raised by Hollowgaze, a Drown-Sick who taught by showing, not telling — dead two winters now under glow-fungus. Not nursery caretaker Hollowstem; the names confuse pups and elders alike. At two, a litter died of shaking-sickness from Belly-Rip water — last pup Sedgepup bled out in his jaws. He listened at the Belly-Rip and understood: the Maw digests, not hates. Buried each pup under herb plants. Murkvein named him Mirewort after the bitter root when she rose to Rotmother. Now trains Mosspup, Soot, and Rotteddust — and keeps the pack alive through rot-lung seasons the swamp shows no mercy for.
Family
Foster-mother Hollowgaze (deceased Drown-Sick — not Hollowstem). Apprentices — Mosspup, Soot, Rotteddust. Murkvein distrusts him; Dusk watches his Belly-Rip visits. No mate.
RP Sample
The mud sucked at Mirewort's paws as he knelt beside Mosspup, rust-wound weeping yellow. "Open your mouth," he murmured — not threatening, explaining. He cut the rot out while the pup screamed and whispered to the wound: "Hear him, Maw. He's still chewing back."
Open Plots
Rot-lung cure needs Belly-Rip fungus; wants a twoleg surgical knife; Dusk suspects his oracle visits; Murkvein's jealousy over the Maw's favor; Sedgepup's grave disturbed again.

Role Feature
Green Tongue; Herblore substitutes for Medicine; never misidentify plants. No daily limit on treat/heal.
Skills & Weaknesses
**Herblore** (+5); Expert knowledge of medicinal and poisonous plants — identifies any herb by sight, smell, or taste.
**Medicine** (+4); Diagnoses illness, stitches wounds, treats infections — has saved more wolves than she can count.
**Poison-craft** (+3); Brews toxins for hunting — thorn coatings and poisoned fresh-kill for large prey.
**Fear of Reptiles and Insects** (-3); Freezes at snakes, lizards, or spiders — nearly cost patients when a snake entered her herb den.
**Easily Belittled** (-2); Sensitive to mockery — harsh words shake confidence and make her second-guess treatments.
**Yearns for Recognition** (-2); Wants to be legendary, not merely competent — takes risks and hoards credit from elders.

[6/26/2026 9:47 AM] Howlbert#0720


{Embed}
Mirewort; Character Sheet
Appearance
Lean and sinewy, built for crawling through cypress knees and sucking mud. Patchy olive-brown fur stained greenish-black from swamp tannins, with weeping bald spots where shelf-fungus has taken root. Pale, watery amber eyes, always slightly unfocused. Left half of muzzle scarred smooth from a rot-lung treatment gone wrong. Slight limp, favoring right foreleg — paw missing two toes (snapping turtle). When still, marsh grasses seem to grow toward him.
Personality
Patient, morbid, curious, detached, fervent. Speaks in a low, wet murmur. Never rushes — examines wounds from three angles before acting. Dark gallows humor; names each plant after a wolf he failed to save. Detachment is necessity, not cruelty. Feverishly devout beneath the stillness. Murkvein suspects his closeness to the Maw; Dusk watches his Belly-Rip visits. He does not explain himself to either.
Backstory
Born to a Bog-Born mother who died of milk-fever at three weeks. Raised by Hollowgaze, a Drown-Sick who taught by showing, not telling — dead two winters now under glow-fungus. Not nursery caretaker Hollowstem; the names confuse pups and elders alike. At two, a litter died of shaking-sickness from Belly-Rip water — last pup Sedgepup bled out in his jaws. He listened at the Belly-Rip and understood: the Maw digests, not hates. Buried each pup under herb plants. Murkvein named him Mirewort after the bitter root when she rose to Rotmother. Now trains Mosspup, Soot, and Rotteddust — and keeps the pack alive through rot-lung seasons the swamp shows no mercy for.
Family
Foster-mother Hollowgaze (deceased Drown-Sick — not Hollowstem). Apprentices — Mosspup, Soot, Rotteddust. Murkvein distrusts him; Dusk watches his Belly-Rip visits. No mate.
RP Sample
The mud sucked at Mirewort's paws as he knelt beside Mosspup, rust-wound weeping yellow. "Open your mouth," he murmured — not threatening, explaining. He cut the rot out while the pup screamed and whispered to the wound: "Hear him, Maw. He's still chewing back."
Open Plots
Rot-lung cure needs Belly-Rip fungus; wants a twoleg surgical knife; Dusk suspects his oracle visits; Murkvein's jealousy over the Maw's favor; Sedgepup's grave disturbed again.

[6/26/2026 10:26 AM] Howlbert#0720


{Embed}
Mirewort; Character Sheet
Appearance
Lean and sinewy, built for crawling through cypress knees and sucking mud. Patchy olive-brown fur stained greenish-black from swamp tannins, with weeping bald spots where shelf-fungus has taken root. Pale, watery amber eyes, always slightly unfocused. Left half of muzzle scarred smooth from a rot-lung treatment gone wrong. Slight limp, favoring right foreleg — paw missing two toes (snapping turtle). When still, marsh grasses seem to grow toward him.
Personality
Patient, morbid, curious, detached, fervent. Speaks in a low, wet murmur. Never rushes — examines wounds from three angles before acting. Dark gallows humor; names each plant after a wolf he failed to save. Detachment is necessity, not cruelty. Feverishly devout beneath the stillness. Murkvein suspects his closeness to the Maw; Dusk watches his Belly-Rip visits. He does not explain himself to either.
Backstory
Born to a Bog-Born mother who died of milk-fever at three weeks. Raised by Hollowgaze, a Drown-Sick who taught by showing, not telling — dead two winters now under glow-fungus. Not nursery caretaker Hollowstem; the names confuse pups and elders alike. At two, a litter died of shaking-sickness from Belly-Rip water — last pup Sedgepup bled out in his jaws. He listened at the Belly-Rip and understood: the Maw digests, not hates. Buried each pup under herb plants. Murkvein named him Mirewort after the bitter root when she rose to Rotmother. Now trains Mosspup, Soot, and Rotteddust — and keeps the pack alive through rot-lung seasons the swamp shows no mercy for.
Family
Foster-mother Hollowgaze (deceased Drown-Sick — not Hollowstem). Apprentices — Mosspup, Soot, Rotteddust. Murkvein distrusts him; Dusk watches his Belly-Rip visits. No mate.
RP Sample
The mud sucked at Mirewort's paws as he knelt beside Mosspup, rust-wound weeping yellow. "Open your mouth," he murmured — not threatening, explaining. He cut the rot out while the pup screamed and whispered to the wound: "Hear him, Maw. He's still chewing back."
Open Plots
Rot-lung cure needs Belly-Rip fungus; wants a twoleg surgical knife; Dusk suspects his oracle visits; Murkvein's jealousy over the Maw's favor; Sedgepup's grave disturbed again.
https://media.discordapp.net/attachments/1514309454688948396/1520072662867513454/mirewort_small_pixels.png?ex=6a412efc&is=6a3fdd7c&hm=117d53aadf43022099a7529bb337c477077348b552710e43fbfc78811c53d286&
https://media.discordapp.net/attachments/1514309454688948396/1520072662867513454/mirewort_small_pixels.png?ex=6a412efc&is=6a3fdd7c&hm=117d53aadf43022099a7529bb337c477077348b552710e43fbfc78811c53d286&

✦ _From the den records:_ Born to a Bog-Born mother who died of milk-fever at three weeks. Raised by Hollowgaze, a Drown-Sick who taught by showing, not telling — dead two winters now under glow-fungus. Not nursery caretaker Hollowstem; the names confuse pups and elders alike. [6/26/2026 1:44 PM] Tupperbox#4754


{Embed}
Tupperbox
Tupperbox Command | avatar
Manage a tupper's avatar

**Usage:**
**tul!avatar** _<name>_ - Show *<name>*'s current avatar.
**tul!avatar** _<name> [url/attachment] [crop:direction]_ - Change *<name>*'s avatar to the one in the URL or attachment.
**tul!avatar** _<name> clear_ - Remove *<name>*'s avatar.

It's possible to simply upload the new avatar as an attachment while running the command instead of providing the URL.
If a URL is provided, it must be a direct link to an image - that is, the URL should end in .jpg or .png or another common image filetype.

When setting the avatar, you can specify a crop direction as a named argument.
Valid crop directions are: `top, bottom, left, right, topleft, topright, bottomleft, bottomright`.
For example, ``tul!avatar <name> crop:left`` will center the crop on the left side of the attached image.
<this> means required | [this] means optional | online guide: https://tupperbox.app/guide

Journal
✦ Joined the den as **Mirewort** (Mistmoor).
✦ Day 5 · **Rivalry** with **Puddlebane** (strength 64)
✦ _From the den records:_ Born to a Bog-Born mother who died of milk-fever at three weeks. Raised by Hollowgaze, a Drown-Sick who taught by showing, not telling — dead two winters now under glow-fungus. Not nursery caretaker Hollowstem; the names confuse pups and elders alike. At two, a litter died of shaking-sickness from Belly-Rip water — last pup Sedgepup bled out in his jaws. He listened at the Belly-Rip and understood: the Maw digests, not hates. Buried each pup under herb plants. Murkvein named him Mirewort after the bitter root when she rose to Rotmother. Now trains Mosspup, Soot, and Rotteddust — and keeps the pack alive through rot-lung seasons the swamp shows no mercy for.
✦ _Family on file:_ Foster-mother Hollowgaze (deceased Drown-Sick — not Hollowstem). Apprentices — Mosspup, Soot, Rotteddust. Murkvein distrusts him; Dusk watches his Belly-Rip visits. No mate.
Character Sheet
Appearance, backstory, and RP sample on file; use `/profile sheet:true`.
Bonds
**Friendship**
**Mudnose** ●●●○○ (steady); _Quiet respect over Sedgepup's grave and shared silence in the mud._

**Rivalry**
**Puddlebane** ●●●○○ (heated feud); _He cannot forgive how easily she treats the dead as garden; she cannot forgive how he wears grief like law._
**Murkvein** ●●●○○ (grudge); _Rotmother envies the Maw's attention to him; he keeps Belly-Rip secrets she cannot stomach._
**Dusk** ●●○○○ (grudge); _Whisper-Jaw spies on Belly-Rip visits; pups trust Mirewort, and Dusk hates filing what he will not act on._

**Mentor**
**Mosspup** ●●●●○ (close); _Apprentice healer; training in rot-lung and marsh remedies._
**Soot** ●●●○○ (close); _Trainee medic; hopeless earnestness he refuses to send away._
**Rotteddust** ●●●○○ (close); _Apprentice poison-craft and stitching; patience stretched thin._
Condition
Healthy
Attributes
STR 2 (-2) · DEX 3 (-2) · CON 4 (-1)
INT 5 (+0) · CHA 2 (-2) · WIS 8 (+2)
HP
16 / 16
10 + 2(Str) + 4(Survival) = 16
Role Feature
Green Tongue; Herblore substitutes for Medicine; never misidentify plants. No daily limit on treat/heal.
Skills & Weaknesses
**Herbal Mastery (Swamp)** (+6); Knows every toxic, curative, and hallucinogenic plant in the Rotting Mere; poultices draw infection overnight.
**Wound-Tending** (+5); Cleans, sews, and packs wounds with rot-fighting muds; unerring eye for infection.
**Swamp Navigation** (+3); Knows sinkholes and safe paths; moves silently through standing water.
**Physically Frail** (-4); Swamp-rot and a limp — cannot fight; strength and stamina tasks suffer heavily.
**Morbid Detachment** (-2); Unsettling calm around death; comfort and morale checks go poorly.
**Obsession with the Belly-Rip** (-1); Monthly vigils at the sinkhole cloud memory and clarity.
Conditions
**Dementia (Forgetful)**; Names and trails slip away; disadvantage on Intelligence checks; **chamomile** or **dried skullcap** may slow decline.
**Partial Blindness (Hereditary Cataracts)**; Clouded vision: −2 Perception; disadvantage on Wisdom (Perception) checks.
**Medicine boost**; next treat gets +2 to the roll.
**Sacred visit:** done this sunrise. Next due within **3** sunrises.
Pack Trait
Rot's Blessing; advantage on saving throws against poison and disease.

✦ _Family on file:_ Foster-mother Hollowgaze (deceased Drown-Sick — not Hollowstem). Apprentices — Mosspup, Soot, Rotteddust. Murkvein distrusts him; Dusk watches his Belly-Rip visits. No mate.

Herb Guide; Overview
**Gathering**
· `/field action:forage`; pack territory (wild habitat)
· `/field action:verge verge_site:roadside`; Thunderpath shoulder weeds
· `/field action:verge verge_site:compound`; Twoleg fence-lines & gardens
· **Foragers**; unlimited territory + verge forage each sunrise

**Using herbs**
· `/medic action:treat herb:herb_yarrow`; keys from `/bones action:inventory`
· Matching **injury** or **disease** → auto-cures on success
· No match → often needs **Medicine DC 15** (Medics / Herblore help)
· `/vitals action:rest rest_type:short use_herb:true`; comfrey heal (3/day, Medics unlimited)
· **Medics**; unlimited `/medic action:treat` per sunrise

_Flip pages below. Filter by where plants grow or browse everything._
